</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS4.p3.11" class="ltx_p">consistent with shot-noise-induced histogram fluctuations propagating through a Lipschitz map <math id="S2.SS4.p3.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\Phi" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Phi</annotation></semantics></math>.
Weighted nonlinear least-squares fits (using empirical standard deviations as weights; fit restricted to <math id="S2.SS4.p3.5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S\geq 75" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>≥</mo><mn>75</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S\geq 75</annotation></semantics></math>) yield
<math id="S2.SS4.p3.6.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\delta_{\infty}=46.68\pm 10.86" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>δ</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mn>46.68</mn><mo>±</mo><mn>10.86</mn></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\delta_{\infty}=46.68\pm 10.86</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S2.SS4.p3.7.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k=236.89\pm 160.35" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mn>236.89</mn><mo>±</mo><mn>160.35</mn></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">k=236.89\pm 160.35</annotation></semantics></math> for EMA-off (<math id="S2.SS4.p3.8.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R^{2}_{w}=0.596" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>R</mi><mi>w</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mn>0.596</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R^{2}_{w}=0.596</annotation></semantics></math>),
and <math id="S2.SS4.p3.9.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\delta_{\infty}=89.05\pm 5.61" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>δ</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∞</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mn>89.05</mn><mo>±</mo><mn>5.61</mn></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\delta_{\infty}=89.05\pm 5.61</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S2.SS4.p3.10.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k=275.75\pm 85.88" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mn>275.75</mn><mo>±</mo><mn>85.88</mn></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">k=275.75\pm 85.88</annotation></semantics></math> for EMA-on (<math id="S2.SS4.p3.11.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R^{2}_{w}=0.901" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msubsup><mi>R</mi><mi>w</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo>=</mo><mn>0.901</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R^{2}_{w}=0.901</annotation></semantics></math>).
The substantially improved goodness-of-fit and higher asymptotic gain under EMA indicate that feature smoothing enlarges the effective operating regime at low-to-moderate shot budgets, mitigating shot-limited fluctuations in the conditioning signal without altering the student architecture. Together, these results support the central prediction of Eq. (<a href="#S2.E14" title="In 2.4 Robustness to shot noise and hardware-relevant perturbations ‣ 2 Results ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">14</span></a>): photonic sampling noise induces a controlled, shot-governed perturbation whose impact can be reduced by simple, hardware-compatible temporal averaging.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S3" class="ltx_section">
<h2 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">3 </span>Conclusion</h2>

<div id="S3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.p1.1" class="ltx_p">PQKD shows that finite-shot continuous-variable photonic processors can be used as training-time resources for practical model compression. By coupling a programmable photonic sampler to photonic-conditioned dictionary convolutions, PQKD replaces dense convolutional kernels with a low-rank spatial basis whose channel mixing is driven by a compact, shot-limited photonic feature, while keeping inference fully classical. Across MNIST, Fashion-MNIST and CIFAR-10, PQKD achieves stable knowledge distillation under progressively stronger convolutional compression and exposes a clear compression–accuracy frontier controlled by the basis rank and photonic parameter budget. The observed shot-noise behaviour and the effectiveness of simple feature smoothing further indicate that PQKD remains usable under realistic sampling constraints, providing a practical route to integrate near-term photonic quantum hardware into parameter-efficient learning pipelines.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4" class="ltx_section">
<h2 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">4 </span>Methods</h2>

<section id="S4.SS1" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">4.1 </span>Datasets and preprocessing</h3>

<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">MNIST.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2" class="ltx_p">We used the MNIST handwritten digit dataset (28<math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\times" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mo>×</mo><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\times</annotation></semantics></math>28 grayscale, 10 classes) as the primary benchmark to quantify compression–accuracy trade-offs under controlled conditions. Images were converted to tensors and rescaled to <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="[0,1]" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">[0,1]</annotation></semantics></math> without additional augmentation. Unless stated otherwise, we constructed fixed splits of <span id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">train/val</span> = <span id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.2" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">45,000/5,000</span> by randomly permuting the canonical MNIST training and test sets using a fixed seed (see <em id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.3" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">Reproducibility</em>). Data loaders used batch size 64 with shuffling enabled for training only.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Fashion-MNIST.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.2" class="ltx_p">To evaluate PQKD beyond digit recognition and to test robustness on more structured visual patterns, we additionally used the Fashion-MNIST dataset, which consists of 28<math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\times" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mo>×</mo><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\times</annotation></semantics></math>28 grayscale images from 10 clothing categories. Preprocessing followed the same protocol as MNIST: images were converted to tensors and rescaled to <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="[0,1]" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">[0,1]</annotation></semantics></math> without data augmentation. We constructed fixed <span id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">train/val</span> splits of <span id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.2" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">45,000/5,000</span> using a fixed random seed, and used identical data-loading settings. Compared to MNIST, Fashion-MNIST exhibits higher intra-class variability and weaker local stroke structure, providing a more challenging test for structured convolutional compression.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">CIFAR-10.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.1" class="ltx_p">To assess scalability to natural images with colour channels and richer spatial statistics, we further evaluated PQKD on the CIFAR-10 dataset, comprising 32<math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\times" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mo>×</mo><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\times</annotation></semantics></math>32 RGB images across 10 object classes. Images were converted to tensors and normalised channel-wise using the standard CIFAR-10 mean and standard deviation. No data augmentation was applied, in order to isolate the effect of architectural compression. We constructed fixed <span id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">train/val</span> splits of <span id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.2" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">45,000/5,000</span> using a fixed seed. For CIFAR-10 experiments, convolutional layers were adjusted to accept three input channels, while all compression mechanisms, photonic feature mappings, and training protocols were otherwise kept identical to the MNIST and Fashion-MNIST settings.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Synthetic dataset.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.2" class="ltx_p">To decouple architectural effects from dataset-specific structure and to stress-test robustness, we additionally created a synthetic 10-class image dataset of size-matched 28<math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\times" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mo>×</mo><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\times</annotation></semantics></math>28 grayscale images. Each class <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c\in\{0,\dots,9\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mn>9</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c\in\{0,\dots,9\}</annotation></semantics></math> is defined by a small set of class-specific Gaussian “ink” templates placed at fixed anchor locations with random jitter:</p>
<ol id="S4.I1" class="ltx_enumerate">
<li id="S4.I1.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">1.</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i1.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Start from a zero image <math id="S4.I1.i1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="I\in\mathbb{R}^{28\times 28}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>I</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mn>28</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>28</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I\in\mathbb{R}^{28\times 28}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I1.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">2.</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i2.p1.8" class="ltx_p">For class <math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>c</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c</annotation></semantics></math>, select <math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>m</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m</annotation></semantics></math> anchors <math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{(\mu_{j}^{(c)},\nu_{j}^{(c)})\}_{j=1}^{m}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msubsup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>μ</mi><mi>j</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>,</mo><msubsup><mi>ν</mi><mi>j</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>m</mi></msubsup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{(\mu_{j}^{(c)},\nu_{j}^{(c)})\}_{j=1}^{m}</annotation></semantics></math> (we used <math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m=2" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>m</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m=2</annotation></semantics></math>–<math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="3" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mn>3</mn><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3</annotation></semantics></math>), apply jitter <math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(\Delta\mu,\Delta\nu)\sim\mathcal{N}(0,\sigma_{\mathrm{jit}}^{2})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>μ</mi></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Δ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>ν</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>∼</mo><mrow><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">𝒩</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><msubsup><mi>σ</mi><mi>jit</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\Delta\mu,\Delta\nu)\sim\mathcal{N}(0,\sigma_{\mathrm{jit}}^{2})</annotation></semantics></math>, and add Gaussian blobs
<math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="I\leftarrow I+\sum_{j=1}^{m}a_{j}\exp\!\left(-\frac{(u-\mu_{j})^{2}+(v-\nu_{j})^{2}}{2\sigma_{\mathrm{blob}}^{2}}\right)," display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>I</mi><mo stretchy="false">←</mo><mrow><mi>I</mi><mo rspace="0.055em">+</mo><mrow><msubsup><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>m</mi></msubsup><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.167em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mpadded style="width:1.370em;" width="1.370em"><mi>exp</mi></mpadded><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>u</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>μ</mi><mi>j</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>v</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>ν</mi><mi>j</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>σ</mi><mi>blob</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow></mfrac></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I\leftarrow I+\sum_{j=1}^{m}a_{j}\exp\!\left(-\frac{(u-\mu_{j})^{2}+(v-\nu_{j})^{2}}{2\sigma_{\mathrm{blob}}^{2}}\right),</annotation></semantics></math>
with amplitudes <math id="S4.I1.i2.p1.8.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="a_{j}\sim\mathrm{Uniform}(0.8,1.2)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>j</mi></msub><mo>∼</mo><mrow><mi>Uniform</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0.8</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>1.2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a_{j}\sim\mathrm{Uniform}(0.8,1.2)</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I1.i3" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">3.</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i3.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Add pixel noise <math id="S4.I1.i3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\epsilon\sim\mathcal{N}(0,\sigma_{\mathrm{pix}}^{2})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi><mo>∼</mo><mrow><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">𝒩</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><msubsup><mi>σ</mi><mi>pix</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon\sim\mathcal{N}(0,\sigma_{\mathrm{pix}}^{2})</annotation></semantics></math> and clip to <math id="S4.I1.i3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="[0,1]" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">[0,1]</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ol>
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.5" class="ltx_p">We used <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\sigma_{\mathrm{blob}}=1.6" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mi>blob</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>1.6</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma_{\mathrm{blob}}=1.6</annotation></semantics></math>, <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\sigma_{\mathrm{jit}}=0.8" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mi>jit</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0.8</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma_{\mathrm{jit}}=0.8</annotation></semantics></math>, and <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.5.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\sigma_{\mathrm{pix}}=0.05" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>σ</mi><mi>pix</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0.05</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sigma_{\mathrm{pix}}=0.05</annotation></semantics></math> unless stated otherwise. The synthetic dataset was class-balanced and split into train/val/test in the same ratios as MNIST. This dataset provides a tunable setting to probe the effect of compression and photonic noise under controlled intra-class variability.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS2" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">4.2 </span>Classical models</h3>

<section id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Teacher CNN.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1.1" class="ltx_p">The teacher is a conventional CNN with three convolutional blocks and a global-average-pooling (GAP) classifier head:</p>
<ul id="S4.I2" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="S4.I2.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i1.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i1.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">conv1:</span> <math id="S4.I2.i1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1\rightarrow c_{1}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1\rightarrow c_{1}</annotation></semantics></math>, kernel <math id="S4.I2.i1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="5\times 5" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>5</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">5\times 5</annotation></semantics></math>, padding 2, ReLU, <math id="S4.I2.i1.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="2\times 2" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2\times 2</annotation></semantics></math> max-pool;</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i2.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i2.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">conv2:</span> <math id="S4.I2.i2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c_{1}\rightarrow c_{2}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_{1}\rightarrow c_{2}</annotation></semantics></math>, kernel <math id="S4.I2.i2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="3\times 3" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>3</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3\times 3</annotation></semantics></math>, padding 1, ReLU, <math id="S4.I2.i2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="2\times 2" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2\times 2</annotation></semantics></math> max-pool;</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i3" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i3.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i3.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">conv3:</span> <math id="S4.I2.i3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c_{2}\rightarrow c_{3}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_{2}\rightarrow c_{3}</annotation></semantics></math>, kernel <math id="S4.I2.i3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="3\times 3" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>3</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3\times 3</annotation></semantics></math>, padding 1, ReLU, dropout (<math id="S4.I2.i3.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p=0.25" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0.25</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p=0.25</annotation></semantics></math>);</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i4" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i4.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i4.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">GAP:</span> adaptive average pooling to <math id="S4.I2.i4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1\times 1" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1\times 1</annotation></semantics></math>;</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i5" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i5.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i5.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">fc:</span> linear layer <math id="S4.I2.i5.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c_{3}\rightarrow 10" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mn>10</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_{3}\rightarrow 10</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.7" class="ltx_p">We report results for multiple teacher widths (e.g., <math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})\in\{(32,64,128),(48,96,128),(64,128,128)\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>32</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>64</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>48</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>96</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>64</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})\in\{(32,64,128),(48,96,128),(64,128,128)\}</annotation></semantics></math>) to control teacher capacity and keep reported compression factors directly comparable across operating points (since the student’s parameterisation is largely fixed by <math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(R_{1},R_{2},R_{3})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(R_{1},R_{2},R_{3})</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>), and to ensure that any performance differences are not an artefact of an over/under-parameterised teacher. With biases enabled and no BatchNorm, the teacher has
<math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=9c_{1}c_{2}+9c_{2}c_{3}+26c_{1}+c_{2}+11c_{3}+10" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>teacher</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mn>9</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mn>9</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mn>26</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><mrow><mn>11</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>10</mn></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=9c_{1}c_{2}+9c_{2}c_{3}+26c_{1}+c_{2}+11c_{3}+10</annotation></semantics></math>
trainable parameters. For the widths used in this work:
<math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})=(32,64,128)\Rightarrow P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=94{,}474" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>32</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>64</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>teacher</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>94</mn></mrow><mo>,</mo><mn>474</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})=(32,64,128)\Rightarrow P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=94{,}474</annotation></semantics></math> ;
<math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})=(48,96,128)\Rightarrow P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=154{,}826" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>48</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>96</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>teacher</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>154</mn></mrow><mo>,</mo><mn>826</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})=(48,96,128)\Rightarrow P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=154{,}826</annotation></semantics></math> ;
<math id="S4.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p2.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})=(64,128,128)\Rightarrow P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=224{,}394." display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>64</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>teacher</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>224</mn></mrow><mo>,</mo><mn>394</mn></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})=(64,128,128)\Rightarrow P_{\mathrm{teacher}}=224{,}394.</annotation></semantics></math></p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS3" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">4.3 </span>Quantum model: Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation</h3>

<section id="S4.SS3.SSS1" class="ltx_subsubsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsubsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsubsection">4.3.1 </span>Photonic circuit, sampling, and continuous-variable setting</h4>

<div id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p1.4" class="ltx_p">PQKD uses a parameterised photonic circuit to generate a compact conditioning vector. We consider a continuous-variable (CV) photonic processor implemented as an integrated optical interferometer with tunable parameters <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> (e.g., phase shifts and beam-splitter angles; optionally including squeezing depending on hardware). For a fixed input state <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\rho_{\mathrm{in}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_{\mathrm{in}}</annotation></semantics></math> over <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>N</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math> modes and a parameterised unitary <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="U(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>U</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>, the output state is</p>
<table id="S4.E16" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E16.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\rho_{\theta}=U(\theta)\,\rho_{\mathrm{in}}\,U(\theta)^{\dagger}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>U</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0.170em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>U</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>†</mo></msup></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_{\theta}=U(\theta)\,\rho_{\mathrm{in}}\,U(\theta)^{\dagger}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(16)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.7" class="ltx_p">Let <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\Omega" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Omega</annotation></semantics></math> denote a finite (or countable) set of measurement outcomes and let
<math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{M_{\omega}\}_{\omega\in\Omega}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>M</mi><mi>ω</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>ω</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{M_{\omega}\}_{\omega\in\Omega}</annotation></semantics></math> be a POVM on the <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>N</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math>-mode Hilbert space, i.e.,
<math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M_{\omega}\succeq 0" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mi>ω</mi></msub><mo>⪰</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M_{\omega}\succeq 0</annotation></semantics></math> for all <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\omega\in\Omega" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>ω</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega\in\Omega</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\sum_{\omega\in\Omega}M_{\omega}=\mathbb{I}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>ω</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>M</mi><mi>ω</mi></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>𝕀</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sum_{\omega\in\Omega}M_{\omega}=\mathbb{I}</annotation></semantics></math>.
Measuring <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\rho_{\theta}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\rho_{\theta}</annotation></semantics></math> with this POVM induces the categorical distribution</p>
<table id="S4.E17" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E17.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p_{\theta}(\omega)=\operatorname{Tr}\!\big[M_{\omega}\,\rho_{\theta}\big],\qquad\omega\in\Omega," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ω</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mpadded style="width:1.032em;" width="1.032em"><mi>Tr</mi></mpadded><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">[</mo><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mi>ω</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>ρ</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub></mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mi>ω</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_{\theta}(\omega)=\operatorname{Tr}\!\big[M_{\omega}\,\rho_{\theta}\big],\qquad\omega\in\Omega,</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(17)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.8" class="ltx_p">from which we obtain i.i.d. samples <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p2.8.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\omega_{1},\ldots,\omega_{S}\sim p_{\theta}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>ω</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>ω</mi><mi>S</mi></msub></mrow><mo>∼</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega_{1},\ldots,\omega_{S}\sim p_{\theta}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p3.4" class="ltx_p">In practice, we obtain <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p3.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> i.i.d. samples <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p3.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\omega_{1},\ldots,\omega_{S}\sim p_{\theta}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>ω</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>ω</mi><mi>S</mi></msub></mrow><mo>∼</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega_{1},\ldots,\omega_{S}\sim p_{\theta}</annotation></semantics></math> (“shots”) per feature evaluation. Experiments reported here use <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p3.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N=16" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>16</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N=16</annotation></semantics></math> modes with a fixed input pattern and shot budget <math id="S4.SS3.SSS1.p3.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> held constant within a run (unless varied for noise studies). The primary backend is a photonic sampler consistent with time-bin / interferometric circuit models; when hardware is unavailable, we use a simulator with the same input/output interface.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS3.SSS2" class="ltx_subsubsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsubsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsubsection">4.3.2 </span>Photonic feature construction</h4>

<div id="S4.SS3.SSS2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS2.p1.3" class="ltx_p">From the <math id="S4.SS3.SSS2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> sampled outcomes, we construct a fixed-length feature vector <math id="S4.SS3.SSS2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)\in\mathbb{R}^{d}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>d</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)\in\mathbb{R}^{d}</annotation></semantics></math> with <math id="S4.SS3.SSS2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d=512" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>512</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d=512</annotation></semantics></math>:</p>
<ol id="S4.I3" class="ltx_enumerate">
<li id="S4.I3.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">1.</span> 
<div id="S4.I3.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I3.i1.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Convert each sample to a length-<math id="S4.I3.i1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>N</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math> binary vector (thresholded occupancy) <math id="S4.I3.i1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="b\in\{0,1\}^{16}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><mn>16</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b\in\{0,1\}^{16}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I3.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">2.</span> 
<div id="S4.I3.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I3.i2.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Split <math id="S4.I3.i2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="b" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>b</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b</annotation></semantics></math> into two 8-bit halves and map each half to an integer index in <math id="S4.I3.i2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{0,\dots,255\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mn>255</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{0,\dots,255\}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I3.i3" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">3.</span> 
<div id="S4.I3.i3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I3.i3.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Form two histograms over <math id="S4.I3.i3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{0,\dots,255\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mn>255</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{0,\dots,255\}</annotation></semantics></math>, normalise them to probability vectors, and concatenate to obtain <math id="S4.I3.i3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z\in\mathbb{R}^{512}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mn>512</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z\in\mathbb{R}^{512}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I3.i4" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">4.</span> 
<div id="S4.I3.i4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I3.i4.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Standardise <math id="S4.I3.i4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>z</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z</annotation></semantics></math> (zero mean, unit variance) and apply a fixed scaling factor to control conditioning magnitude.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ol>
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS2.p1.4" class="ltx_p">This marginal-based representation is intentionally low-variance under finite shots and yields a stable conditioning signal without requiring differentiation through the photonic sampler.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS3.SSS3" class="ltx_subsubsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsubsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsubsection">4.3.3 </span>Compressed convolution via photonic-conditioned dictionary mixing</h4>

<div id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.7" class="ltx_p">Each compressed convolutional layer replaces a fully trainable kernel tensor
<math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times k\times k}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times k\times k}</annotation></semantics></math>
by a dictionary model that separates <em id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.7.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">spatial structure</em> from <em id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.7.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">channel mixing</em>.
Specifically, we introduce <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> trainable spatial basis filters
<math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k\times k}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k\times k}</annotation></semantics></math> and a channel-mixing tensor
<math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times R}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>R</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times R}</annotation></semantics></math> such that, for each output channel <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="o" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>o</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">o</annotation></semantics></math>,
input channel <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="i" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>i</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math>, and spatial indices <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\alpha,\beta\in\{1,\ldots,k\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>α</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha,\beta\in\{1,\ldots,k\}</annotation></semantics></math>,</p>
<table id="S4.E18" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E18.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{o,i,\alpha,\beta}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}M_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,\alpha,\beta}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>α</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow></msub><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>R</mi></munderover><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>α</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>β</mi></mrow></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{o,i,\alpha,\beta}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}M_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,\alpha,\beta}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(18)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.8" class="ltx_p">Equivalently, using slice notation one may write
<math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p1.8.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}M_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,:,:}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow></msub><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><msubsup><mo>∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>R</mi></msubsup><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}M_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,:,:}</annotation></semantics></math>, but
Eq. (<a href="#S4.E18" title="In 4.3.3 Compressed convolution via photonic-conditioned dictionary mixing ‣ 4.3 Quantum model: Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation ‣ 4 Methods ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">18</span></a>) makes the index structure explicit.</p>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.1" class="ltx_p">Rather than learning <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> directly, PQKD constrains it through the photonic feature:</p>
<table id="S4.E19" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E19.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M)=A\,z(\theta)," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0.170em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M)=A\,z(\theta),</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(19)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.5" class="ltx_p">where <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}R)\times d}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>R</mi></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>d</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}R)\times d}</annotation></semantics></math> is fixed at initialisation (Gaussian i.i.d. entries with variance <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1/d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>/</mo><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1/d</annotation></semantics></math>) and is <em id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.5.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">not</em> trained. The student therefore learns only the basis filters <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>B</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math> (and biases) in the compressed layers, while the photonic module controls channel mixing via <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.p2.5.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
<section id="S4.SS3.SSS3.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Layer compression configurations.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS3.SSS3.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS3.Px1.p1.3" class="ltx_p">We used three configurations to probe scaling:</p>
<ol id="S4.I4" class="ltx_enumerate">
<li id="S4.I4.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">1.</span> 
<div id="S4.I4.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I4.i1.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I4.i1.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Compress conv1 only:</span> replace conv1 by the photonic-conditioned dictionary layer; keep conv2–conv3 dense.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I4.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">2.</span> 
<div id="S4.I4.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I4.i2.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I4.i2.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Compress conv1+conv2:</span> replace conv1 and conv2; keep conv3 dense.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I4.i3" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">3.</span> 
<div id="S4.I4.i3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I4.i3.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I4.i3.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Compress all convs:</span> replace conv1–conv3; keep GAP+fc dense.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ol>
<p id="S4.SS3.SSS3.Px1.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Each compressed layer has its own basis rank <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.Px1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{\ell}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\ell}</annotation></semantics></math> (e.g., <math id="S4.SS3.SSS3.Px1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{1},R_{2},R_{3}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{1},R_{2},R_{3}</annotation></semantics></math>), and we swept these ranks to trace compression frontiers.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS4" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">4.4 </span>Training objective and optimisation</h3>

<section id="S4.SS4.SSS1" class="ltx_subsubsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsubsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsubsection">4.4.1 </span>Knowledge distillation loss</h4>

<div id="S4.SS4.SSS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS4.SSS1.p1.4" class="ltx_p">Teacher logits are denoted <math id="S4.SS4.SSS1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="t(x)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t(x)</annotation></semantics></math> and student logits <math id="S4.SS4.SSS1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="s(x;w,\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>;</mo><mi>w</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">s(x;w,\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>. With temperature <math id="S4.SS4.SSS1.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\tau" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>τ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\tau</annotation></semantics></math> and mixing coefficient <math id="S4.SS4.SSS1.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\lambda" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>λ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\lambda</annotation></semantics></math>, we minimise</p>
<table id="S4.E20" class="ltx_equationgroup ltx_eqn_table">
<tbody>
<tr id="S4.E20X" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_right ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="S4.E20X.2.1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{KD}}(w,\theta)=" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi><mi>KD</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>w</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi></mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\displaystyle\mathcal{L}_{\mathrm{KD}}(w,\theta)=</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="S4.E20X.3.2.2.m1" class="ltx_math_unparsed" alttext="\displaystyle\ \mathbb{E}_{(x,y)}\Big[\lambda\,\mathrm{CE}\!\big(y,\ \mathrm{softmax}(s(x;w,\theta))\big)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>𝔼</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">[</mo><mi>λ</mi><mpadded style="width:1.412em;" width="1.412em"><mi>CE</mi></mpadded><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mi>softmax</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>s</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>;</mo><mi>w</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\displaystyle\ \mathbb{E}_{(x,y)}\Big[\lambda\,\mathrm{CE}\!\big(y,\ \mathrm{softmax}(s(x;w,\theta))\big)</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>

</tr>
<tr id="S4.E20Xa" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="S4.E20Xa.2.1.1.m1" class="ltx_math_unparsed" alttext="\displaystyle\quad+(1-\lambda)\,\tau^{2}\,\mathrm{KL}\!\Big(\mathrm{softmax}\!\big(\tfrac{t(x)}{\tau}\big)\ \Big\|\ \mathrm{softmax}\!\big(\tfrac{s(x;w,\theta)}{\tau}\big)\Big)\Big]." display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>λ</mi><mo rspace="0.170em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msup><mi>τ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mpadded style="width:1.431em;" width="1.431em"><mi>KL</mi></mpadded><mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">(</mo><mpadded style="width:3.720em;" width="3.720em"><mi>softmax</mi></mpadded><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">(</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mi>τ</mi></mfrac><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em" rspace="0.222em">)</mo></mrow><mo mathsize="1.600em" rspace="0.667em">∥</mo><mpadded style="width:3.720em;" width="3.720em"><mi>softmax</mi></mpadded><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">(</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>;</mo><mi>w</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mi>τ</mi></mfrac><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">)</mo></mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">)</mo></mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">]</mo><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\displaystyle\quad+(1-\lambda)\,\tau^{2}\,\mathrm{KL}\!\Big(\mathrm{softmax}\!\big(\tfrac{t(x)}{\tau}\big)\ \Big\|\ \mathrm{softmax}\!\big(\tfrac{s(x;w,\theta)}{\tau}\big)\Big)\Big].</annotation></semantics></math></td>
