</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1.9" class="ltx_p">where <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1.6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="*" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mo>∗</mo><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">*</annotation></semantics></math> denotes spatial convolution and <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1.7.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{o,i}\in\mathbb{R}^{k\times k}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{o,i}\in\mathbb{R}^{k\times k}</annotation></semantics></math> is the kernel slice coupling input channel <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1.8.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="i" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>i</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">i</annotation></semantics></math> to output channel <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px1.p1.9.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="o" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>o</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">o</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Dictionary factorisation of kernels.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.2" class="ltx_p">PQKD replaces the dense kernel <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>W</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W</annotation></semantics></math> by a dictionary (basis) of <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> spatial filters and a set of channel mixing coefficients. Specifically, introduce trainable basis filters</p>
<table id="S2.E16" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">

<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S16)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.7" class="ltx_p">and mixing coefficients</p>
<table id="S2.E17" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">

</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.8" class="ltx_p">such that each channel-to-channel kernel is expressed as a linear combination of the shared basis:</p>
<table id="S2.E18" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E18.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}M_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,:,:}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow></msub><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>R</mi></munderover><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}M_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,:,:}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S18)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.6" class="ltx_p">Equation (<a href="#S2.E18" title="In Dictionary factorisation of kernels. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S18</span></a>) is a <em id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.6.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">structured</em> parameterisation: spatial degrees of freedom are concentrated in the basis <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>B</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math>, while channel coupling is handled by <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math>. If <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.5.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R\ll C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>≪</mo><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R\ll C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}</annotation></semantics></math>, this can drastically reduce the number of trainable parameters <em id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.6.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">provided that</em> <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px2.p1.6.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> itself is not fully trainable.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Photonic-conditioned mixing (core PQKD mechanism).</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.3" class="ltx_p">The key idea in PQKD is to avoid training the full mixing tensor <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math>. Instead, <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> is generated deterministically from the photonic feature <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)\in\mathbb{R}^{d}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>d</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)\in\mathbb{R}^{d}</annotation></semantics></math> via a fixed linear map:</p>
<table id="S2.E19" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E19.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M)=A\,z(\theta),\qquad A\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}R)\times d}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0.170em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>R</mi></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>d</mi></mrow></msup></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M)=A\,z(\theta),\qquad A\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}R)\times d}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S19)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.9" class="ltx_p">Here <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(\cdot)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">⋅</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(\cdot)</annotation></semantics></math> denotes vectorisation that stacks all entries of <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> into a column vector. The matrix <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.6.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> is <em id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.9.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">fixed</em> (sampled once using a prescribed random seed and then held constant) and is therefore excluded from trainable parameter counts. Under this construction, the channel mixing coefficients <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.7.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> are not free parameters; they vary only through the <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.8.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math>-dimensional photonic control signal <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p1.9.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.1" class="ltx_p">For implementation, one typically reshapes <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="Az(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Az(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> back into the tensor form</p>
<table id="S2.E20" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E20.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M(z)=\mathrm{reshape}\big(Az,\ [C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}},R]\big)." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>reshape</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">(</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M(z)=\mathrm{reshape}\big(Az,\ [C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}},R]\big).</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S20)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.3" class="ltx_p">Combining Eq. (<a href="#S2.E18" title="In Dictionary factorisation of kernels. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S18</span></a>) with Eq. (<a href="#S2.E20" title="In Photonic-conditioned mixing (core PQKD mechanism). ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S20</span></a>) yields an explicit mapping from <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> and the basis <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>B</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math> to the full kernel:</p>
<table id="S2.E21" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E21.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W(z,B)_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}\Big(\mathrm{reshape}(Az,\ [C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}},R])\Big)_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,:,:}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false" rspace="0em">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>R</mi></munderover><mrow><msub><mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">(</mo><mrow><mi>reshape</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W(z,B)_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R}\Big(\mathrm{reshape}(Az,\ [C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}},R])\Big)_{o,i,r}\,B_{r,:,:}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S21)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.5" class="ltx_p">In other words, <em id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.5.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">all</em> channel mixing across the layer is confined to the <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math>-dimensional subspace <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px3.p2.5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{Az:z\in\mathbb{R}^{d}\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>d</mi></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{Az:z\in\mathbb{R}^{d}\}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Equivalent matrix formulation.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.4" class="ltx_p">Let <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{(k)}\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}})\times k^{2}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{(k)}\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}})\times k^{2}}</annotation></semantics></math> denote the kernel tensor flattened over spatial dimensions, and let <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B_{(k)}\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k^{2}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B_{(k)}\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k^{2}}</annotation></semantics></math> denote the basis filters flattened similarly. Define <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M_{(c)}\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}})\times R}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>R</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M_{(c)}\in\mathbb{R}^{(C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}})\times R}</annotation></semantics></math> as the mixing matrix obtained by flattening the first two indices of <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math>. Then Eq. (<a href="#S2.E18" title="In Dictionary factorisation of kernels. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S18</span></a>) is equivalent to</p>
<table id="S2.E22" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E22.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{(k)}=M_{(c)}\,B_{(k)}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{(k)}=M_{(c)}\,B_{(k)}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S22)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.7" class="ltx_p">Equation (<a href="#S2.E19" title="In Photonic-conditioned mixing (core PQKD mechanism). ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S19</span></a>) specifies that <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M_{(c)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M_{(c)}</annotation></semantics></math> lies in a <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math>-dimensional linear subspace parameterised by <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.7.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>. This makes explicit how PQKD imposes a <em id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px4.p1.7.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">low-dimensional manifold</em> constraint on the kernel space.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Forward computation.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Given <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> and basis filters <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>B</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math>, the layer computes:</p>
<ol id="S2.I1" class="ltx_enumerate">
<li id="S2.I1.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">1.</span> 
<div id="S2.I1.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.I1.i1.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Generate <math id="S2.I1.i1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M\leftarrow\mathrm{reshape}(Az(\theta),[C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}},R])" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">←</mo><mrow><mi>reshape</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M\leftarrow\mathrm{reshape}(Az(\theta),[C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}},R])</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S2.I1.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">2.</span> 
<div id="S2.I1.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.I1.i2.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Form the effective kernel using Eq. (<a href="#S2.E18" title="In Dictionary factorisation of kernels. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S18</span></a>).</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S2.I1.i3" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">3.</span> 
<div id="S2.I1.i3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.I1.i3.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Apply convolution as in Eq. (<a href="#S2.E15a" title="In Standard convolution. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S15</span></a>).</p>
</div>
</li>
</ol>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1.4" class="ltx_p">In practice, step (2) can be implemented efficiently via tensor contractions. One convenient expression is</p>
<table id="S2.E23" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E23.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W(z,B)=\mathrm{einsum}\big(\texttt{oir,rxy}\rightarrow\texttt{oixy},\ M(z),\ B\big)," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>einsum</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">(</mo><mrow><mtext class="ltx_mathvariant_monospace">oir,rxy</mtext><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mtext class="ltx_mathvariant_monospace">oixy</mtext><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow></mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W(z,B)=\mathrm{einsum}\big(\texttt{oir,rxy}\rightarrow\texttt{oixy},\ M(z),\ B\big),</annotation></semantics></math></td>

<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S23)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1.3" class="ltx_p">followed by a standard convolution call <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px5.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{conv2d}(x,W,b,\mathrm{padding}=p_{\mathrm{pad}})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>conv2d</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>W</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>padding</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>pad</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{conv2d}(x,W,b,\mathrm{padding}=p_{\mathrm{pad}})</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Trainable-parameter accounting and compression ratio.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.5" class="ltx_p">For a single compressed convolution layer, the trainable parameters are:</p>
<table id="S2.E24" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E24.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{train}}=\underbrace{Rk^{2}}_{\text{basis }B}+\underbrace{C_{\mathrm{out}}}_{\text{bias}}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>train</mi></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><munder><munder accentunder="true"><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mrow><mtext>basis </mtext><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow></munder><mo>+</mo><munder><munder accentunder="true"><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mtext>bias</mtext></munder></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{train}}=\underbrace{Rk^{2}}_{\text{basis }B}+\underbrace{C_{\mathrm{out}}}_{\text{bias}},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S24)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.2" class="ltx_p">plus the photonic parameter budget <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> if <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> is included in the overall student budget. In contrast, a dense convolution has</p>
<table id="S2.E25" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E25.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{dense}}=C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>dense</mi></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{dense}}=C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S25)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.6" class="ltx_p">Ignoring bias terms for intuition, the per-layer trainable-parameter compression factor is approximately</p>
<table id="S2.E26" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E26.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{layer}}\approx\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}}{Rk^{2}}=\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}}{R},\qquad(R\ll C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}})." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>CR</mi><mi>layer</mi></msub><mo>≈</mo><mfrac><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub></mrow><mi>R</mi></mfrac></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>≪</mo><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{layer}}\approx\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}}{Rk^{2}}=\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}}{R},\qquad(R\ll C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}).</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S26)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.4" class="ltx_p">When multiple layers share the same photonic feature <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> (as in our implementation), <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> becomes a <em id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px6.p1.4.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">shared</em> overhead that does not scale with layer width, which is advantageous when compressing multiple convolutional layers simultaneously.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Interpretation and relation to hypernetworks.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.7" class="ltx_p">Equation (<a href="#S2.E19" title="In Photonic-conditioned mixing (core PQKD mechanism). ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S19</span></a>) can be viewed as a constrained hypernetwork that generates convolutional mixing coefficients from a compact input <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>. The constraint that the generator is linear and fixed (through <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math>) intentionally shifts learning capacity away from the generator and into (i) the trainable basis <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> and (ii) the photonic parameters <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> that control <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> through the sampling-based feature map (Supplementary Note <a href="#S2.SS1a" title="S2.1 Photonic quantum feature map ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S2.1</span></a>). This design choice reduces trainable degrees of freedom, improves reproducibility, and makes the photonic contribution explicit and measurable through the dependence on <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> and the shot budget <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px7.p1.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Extension to multiple compressed layers.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.5" class="ltx_p">For a network with multiple compressed convolutional layers <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ell\in\mathcal{L}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ell\in\mathcal{L}</annotation></semantics></math>, each layer has its own <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{in}},C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}},k_{\ell},R_{\ell})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>,</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{in}},C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}},k_{\ell},R_{\ell})</annotation></semantics></math>, basis <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math>, and fixed projection <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math>, while sharing the same <math id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>:</p>
<table id="S2.E27" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E27.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,B^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><msubsup><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub></munderover><mrow><msubsup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>B</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,B^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S27)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS2.SSS0.Px8.p1.6" class="ltx_p">This yields a coherent mechanism to study “compress conv1”, “compress conv1+conv2”, and “compress all convs” settings under a unified control signal and parameter-counting convention.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS3a" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S2.3 </span>Compression configurations</h3>

<div id="S2.SS3a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3a.p1.1" class="ltx_p">To quantify how PQKD scales with compression strength and network depth, we consider three structured compression regimes that progressively replace larger fractions of the convolutional stack by photonic-conditioned dictionary convolutions (Supplementary Note <a href="#S2.SS2a" title="S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S2.2</span></a>). Throughout, the teacher network uses standard dense convolutions, while the student network matches the teacher macro-architecture (same number of blocks, pooling schedule, and head) but substitutes selected convolution layers by the PQKD parameterisation. This design isolates the effect of structured parameterisation and the photonic conditioning signal from confounding architectural changes.</p>
</div>
<section id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Regime I: compress <span id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv1</span> only.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.1" class="ltx_p">In this regime, only the first convolution layer is replaced by the photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution:</p>
<table id="S2.E28" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E28.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M^{(1)})=A^{(1)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(1)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{1}}M^{(1)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(1)}_{r,:,:}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><msubsup><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></munderover><mrow><msubsup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M^{(1)})=A^{(1)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(1)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{1}}M^{(1)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(1)}_{r,:,:}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S28)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.2" class="ltx_p">All subsequent convolutions (e.g., <span id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv2</span> and <span id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.2" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv3</span>) remain dense and fully trainable. This setting represents a conservative compression strategy that primarily reduces parameters near the input while leaving downstream representational capacity largely intact. It provides a baseline to test whether PQKD can compress early feature extraction without destabilising training.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Regime II: compress <span id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv1+conv2</span>.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Here, both the first and second convolution layers are replaced by PQKD layers with (potentially distinct) basis ranks <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{1}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{1}</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{2}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>R</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{2}</annotation></semantics></math>:</p>
<table id="S2.E29" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E29.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:},\qquad\ell\in\{1,2\}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S29)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.3" class="ltx_p">The third convolution remains dense. This regime substantially increases the fraction of trainable convolution parameters controlled by <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> while still retaining one fully trainable convolution block to absorb residual modelling error. Empirically, this intermediate regime often yields a favourable trade-off between compression and accuracy because it compresses a large portion of the convolutional stack while maintaining a flexible downstream adaptation layer.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Regime III: compress all convolution layers (<span id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv1--conv3</span>).</h5>

<div id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.7" class="ltx_p">In the most aggressive setting, <em id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.7.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">all</em> convolution layers are replaced by photonic-conditioned dictionary convolutions:</p>
<table id="S2.E30" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E30.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:},\qquad\ell\in\{1,2,3\}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mrow><msubsup><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi movablelimits="false">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:},\qquad\ell\in\{1,2,3\}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S30)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.6" class="ltx_p">This regime tests large-scale structured compression, in which the convolutional feature extractor is entirely restricted to the PQKD manifold defined by <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{A^{(\ell)}z(\theta)\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{A^{(\ell)}z(\theta)\}</annotation></semantics></math> and the trainable bases <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{S^{(\ell)}\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{S^{(\ell)}\}</annotation></semantics></math>. Since the same <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> conditions every compressed layer, the photonic parameters <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> act as a <em id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.6.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">shared global control</em> over the entire convolutional stack, while each layer retains local spatial expressivity through its basis <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math> and rank <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{\ell}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\ell}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Rank selection and interpretability.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.8" class="ltx_p">Each compressed layer <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ell" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ell</annotation></semantics></math> has an associated basis rank <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{\ell}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\ell}</annotation></semantics></math>, which controls the number of spatial basis filters in that layer. Intuitively, larger <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{\ell}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\ell}</annotation></semantics></math> increases the spatial expressivity of the reconstructed kernels (Eq. (<a href="#S2.E18" title="In Dictionary factorisation of kernels. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S18</span></a>)) at the cost of more trainable parameters (<math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R_{\ell}k_{\ell}^{2}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>k</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\ell}k_{\ell}^{2}</annotation></semantics></math>). In contrast, the channel mixing degrees of freedom remain confined to the <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math>-dimensional subspace induced by <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A^{(\ell)}z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A^{(\ell)}z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> (Eq. (<a href="#S2.E19" title="In Photonic-conditioned mixing (core PQKD mechanism). ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S19</span></a>)). Our sweep studies therefore treat <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{R_{\ell}\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{R_{\ell}\}</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.8.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> as primary compression knobs.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Parameter accounting across regimes.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.1" class="ltx_p">For a student model with compressed layers <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathcal{L}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}</annotation></semantics></math>, the total trainable parameters are</p>
<table id="S2.E31" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S2.E31.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}=\sum_{\ell\in\mathcal{L}}\big(R_{\ell}k_{\ell}^{2}+C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}}\big)+\sum_{\ell\notin\mathcal{L}}\big(C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}}C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{in}}k_{\ell}^{2}+C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}}\big)+\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}+\dim(\theta)," mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em">+</mo><mrow><munder><mo movablelimits="false" rspace="0em">∑</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>∉</mo><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi></mrow></munder><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">(</mo><mrow><mrow><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>k</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>head</mi></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}=\sum_{\ell\in\mathcal{L}}\big(R_{\ell}k_{\ell}^{2}+C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}}\big)+\sum_{\ell\notin\mathcal{L}}\big(C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}}C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{in}}k_{\ell}^{2}+C^{(\ell)}_{\mathrm{out}}\big)+\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}+\dim(\theta),</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S31)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.3" class="ltx_p">where <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>head</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}</annotation></semantics></math> denotes the parameters of the non-convolutional head (e.g., global-average-pooling classifier). We report both an <em id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.3.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">overall</em> compression ratio (teacher parameters divided by student parameters, including <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>) and a <em id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px5.p1.3.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">conv-only</em> compression ratio restricted to the convolutional layers, to disentangle compression achieved in the feature extractor from contributions of the classifier head.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Practical implementation.</h5>

<div id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1.5" class="ltx_p">In all regimes, each compressed layer uses its own fixed projection matrix <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math> (sampled once and held constant) and its own trainable basis <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math>, while sharing the same photonic feature vector <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> across layers. This choice keeps the student trainable parameter count low and makes the effect of <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> and the shot budget <math id="S2.SS3.SSS0.Px6.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> directly comparable across compression regimes.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S3a" class="ltx_section">
<h2 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">S3 </span>Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability</h2>

<section id="S3.SS1" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S3.1 </span>Trainable-parameter accounting</h3>

<div id="S3.SS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.p1.1" class="ltx_p">To report compression ratios consistently, we distinguish <em id="S3.SS1.p1.1.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">trainable</em> parameters (those updated by learning) from <em id="S3.SS1.p1.1.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">fixed</em> parameters (constants sampled once and held throughout training). This distinction is essential for PQKD because the channel-mixing generator uses a fixed projection matrix <math id="S3.SS1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> (Eq. (<a href="#S2.E19" title="In Photonic-conditioned mixing (core PQKD mechanism). ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S19</span></a>)), which can be large in memory but does not contribute to the number of learnable degrees of freedom.</p>
</div>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Dense convolution (baseline).</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.3" class="ltx_p">A standard 2D convolution with kernel size <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k\times k" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">k\times k</annotation></semantics></math>, <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C_{\mathrm{in}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{\mathrm{in}}</annotation></semantics></math> input channels and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C_{\mathrm{out}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{\mathrm{out}}</annotation></semantics></math> output channels has trainable parameters</p>
<table id="S3.E32" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E32.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{dense}}=C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>dense</mi></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{dense}}=C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S32)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.5" class="ltx_p">where the first term is the weight tensor <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times k\times k}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times k\times k}</annotation></semantics></math> and the second term is the bias vector <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="b\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">PQKD compressed convolution.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.5" class="ltx_p">In PQKD, a compressed convolution layer uses trainable spatial basis filters
<math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k\times k}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k\times k}</annotation></semantics></math> and a bias <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="b\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}}</annotation></semantics></math>, while the channel mixing coefficients are generated deterministically as <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M)=Az(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M)=Az(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> with fixed <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> and photonic feature <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>.
Therefore, the trainable parameters <em id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.5.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">per compressed layer</em> are</p>
<table id="S3.E33" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E33.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{PQKD\ layer}}=\underbrace{Rk^{2}}_{\text{basis }B}+\underbrace{C_{\mathrm{out}}}_{\text{bias}}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mrow><mi>PQKD</mi><mo lspace="0.400em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>layer</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><munder><munder accentunder="true"><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mrow><mtext>basis </mtext><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow></munder><mo>+</mo><munder><munder accentunder="true"><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo stretchy="true">⏟</mo></munder><mtext>bias</mtext></munder></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{PQKD\ layer}}=\underbrace{Rk^{2}}_{\text{basis }B}+\underbrace{C_{\mathrm{out}}}_{\text{bias}},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S33)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.6" class="ltx_p">and this count is independent of <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C_{\mathrm{in}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{\mathrm{in}}</annotation></semantics></math> because channel mixing is not learned directly.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Global photonic parameter budget.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.2" class="ltx_p">The photonic parameters <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta\in\mathbb{R}^{\dim(\theta)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>θ</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta\in\mathbb{R}^{\dim(\theta)}</annotation></semantics></math> are shared across all compressed layers through the feature vector <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>. When reporting <em id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.2.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">overall</em> student trainable parameters, we include this shared budget once:</p>
<table id="S3.E34" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E34.m1" class="ltx_Math" display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>student</mi></msub></mrow><mo movablelimits="false" rspace="0em">∑</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>∉</mo><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi></mrow></munder><mrow><mo maxsize="1.200em" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>head</mi></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}=\sum_{\ell\in\mathcal{L}}\big(R_{\ell}k_{\ell}^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}\big)+\sum_{\ell\notin\mathcal{L}}\big(C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}C_{\mathrm{in}}^{(\ell)}k_{\ell}^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}\big)+\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}+\dim(\theta),</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S34)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.4" class="ltx_p">where <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathcal{L}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}</annotation></semantics></math> denotes the set of compressed convolution layers and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>head</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{head}}</annotation></semantics></math> denotes any non-convolutional parameters (e.g., the GAP classifier head).</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Per-layer compression factor.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.1" class="ltx_p">A useful diagnostic is the per-layer trainable-parameter compression factor, obtained by comparing Eq. (<a href="#S3.E32" title="In Dense convolution (baseline). ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S32</span></a>) and Eq. (<a href="#S3.E33" title="In PQKD compressed convolution. ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S33</span></a>). Ignoring the shared <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> overhead (which is amortised across layers), we define</p>
<table id="S3.E35" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E35.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{conv}}=\frac{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{dense}}}{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{PQKD\ layer}}}\approx\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}}{Rk^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}}=\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}(C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+1)}{Rk^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}}." display="block"
