layer}}}\approx\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}}{Rk^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}}=\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}(C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}+1)}{Rk^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S35)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.3" class="ltx_p">When <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}\gg C_{\mathrm{out}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mo>≫</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}k^{2}\gg C_{\mathrm{out}}</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="Rk^{2}\gg C_{\mathrm{out}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mo>≫</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Rk^{2}\gg C_{\mathrm{out}}</annotation></semantics></math> (a common regime for moderate-to-large channel counts), this simplifies to the intuitive approximation</p>
<table id="S3.E36" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E36.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{conv}}\approx\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}}{R}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>CR</mi><mi>conv</mi></msub><mo>≈</mo><mfrac><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub></mrow><mi>R</mi></mfrac></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{conv}}\approx\frac{C_{\mathrm{out}}C_{\mathrm{in}}}{R}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S36)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.4" class="ltx_p">This highlights the role of <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px4.p1.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> as the primary knob controlling trainable degrees of freedom in the compressed convolution.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px5" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Reporting conventions used in this work.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px5.p1.2" class="ltx_p">We report two complementary ratios:</p>
<ul id="S3.I1" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="S3.I1.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S3.I1.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.I1.i1.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S3.I1.i1.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Conv-only ratio:</span> computed by restricting Eq. (<a href="#S3.E34" title="In Global photonic parameter budget. ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S34</span></a>) to convolution layers only. This isolates compression achieved in the feature extractor.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S3.I1.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S3.I1.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.I1.i2.p1.2" class="ltx_p"><span id="S3.I1.i2.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Overall ratio (including <math id="S3.I1.i2.p1.1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math>):</span> computed using Eq. (<a href="#S3.E34" title="In Global photonic parameter budget. ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S34</span></a>), including <math id="S3.I1.i2.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> once, to reflect the full trainable budget required by PQKD.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px5.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Fixed projection matrices <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px5.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{A^{(\ell)}\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{A^{(\ell)}\}</annotation></semantics></math> are excluded from trainable counts throughout because they are not updated during training; however, we note that they can contribute to memory footprint and can be implemented implicitly (e.g., via structured random features) if memory becomes a constraint.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Mixing subspace induced by a fixed generator.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.2" class="ltx_p">For a given layer with mixing tensor <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times R}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>R</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M\in\mathbb{R}^{C_{\mathrm{out}}\times C_{\mathrm{in}}\times R}</annotation></semantics></math>, define <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m=\mathrm{vec}(M)\in\mathbb{R}^{p}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>m</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>p</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m=\mathrm{vec}(M)\in\mathbb{R}^{p}</annotation></semantics></math> where</p>
<table id="S3.E37" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">

<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.8" class="ltx_p">If <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> has full column rank (a typical case when <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d\leq p" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>p</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d\leq p</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.7.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> is drawn from a continuous distribution), then <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px6.p1.8.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\mathrm{Range}(A))=d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\mathrm{Range}(A))=d</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Best achievable approximation to a target mixing.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Let <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M^{\star}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>M</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M^{\star}</annotation></semantics></math> denote an arbitrary target mixing tensor (e.g., the mixing that would reproduce a desired dense kernel given a fixed basis). Let <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m^{\star}=\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})\in\mathbb{R}^{p}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>m</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>p</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m^{\star}=\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})\in\mathbb{R}^{p}</annotation></semantics></math>. The best approximation within the PQKD subspace is the solution of the least-squares problem</p>
<table id="S3.E40" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E40.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z^{\star}=\arg\min_{z\in\mathbb{R}^{d}}\|m^{\star}-Az\|_{2}^{2}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msup><mi>z</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>arg</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mrow><munder><mi>min</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>d</mi></msup></mrow></munder><mo>⁡</mo><msubsup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mrow><msup><mi>m</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z^{\star}=\arg\min_{z\in\mathbb{R}^{d}}\|m^{\star}-Az\|_{2}^{2}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S40)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.3" class="ltx_p">When <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> has full column rank, the minimiser is unique and given by</p>
<table id="S3.E41" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E41.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z^{\star}=(A^{\top}A)^{-1}A^{\top}m^{\star}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msup><mi>z</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mo>⊤</mo></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>A</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mo>⊤</mo></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>m</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z^{\star}=(A^{\top}A)^{-1}A^{\top}m^{\star},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S41)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.5" class="ltx_p">and the corresponding attainable mixing is the orthogonal projection of <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m^{\star}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>m</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">m^{\star}</annotation></semantics></math> onto <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{Range}(A)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{Range}(A)</annotation></semantics></math>:</p>
<table id="S3.E42" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E42.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="Az^{\star}=\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}\,m^{\star},\qquad\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}:=A(A^{\top}A)^{-1}A^{\top}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>z</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Π</mi><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>m</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Π</mi><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msub><mo>:=</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mo>⊤</mo></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>A</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>A</mi><mo>⊤</mo></msup></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Az^{\star}=\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}\,m^{\star},\qquad\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}:=A(A^{\top}A)^{-1}A^{\top}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S42)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.8" class="ltx_p">The residual <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\|m^{\star}-Az^{\star}\|_{2}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mrow><msup><mi>m</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>z</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|m^{\star}-Az^{\star}\|_{2}</annotation></semantics></math> quantifies the <em id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.8.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">subspace approximation error</em> introduced by restricting <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.7.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> to <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px7.p1.8.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{Range}(A)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{Range}(A)</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Implications for expressivity and the role of <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math>.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.7" class="ltx_p">Two independent design choices control the representational capacity of a compressed convolution:</p>
<ul id="S3.I2" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="S3.I2.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S3.I2.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.I2.i1.p1.5" class="ltx_p"><span id="S3.I2.i1.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Mixing dimension <math id="S3.I2.i1.p1.1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math>:</span> Increasing <math id="S3.I2.i1.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math> enlarges <math id="S3.I2.i1.p1.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{Range}(A)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{Range}(A)</annotation></semantics></math> and reduces the best-case subspace approximation error in Eq. (<a href="#S3.E42" title="In Best achievable approximation to a target mixing. ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S42</span></a>), enabling richer channel coupling patterns across <math id="S3.I2.i1.p1.4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(C_{\mathrm{out}},C_{\mathrm{in}})</annotation></semantics></math> for a fixed rank <math id="S3.I2.i1.p1.5.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S3.I2.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S3.I2.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.I2.i2.p1.5" class="ltx_p"><span id="S3.I2.i2.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Basis rank <math id="S3.I2.i2.p1.1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math>:</span> Increasing <math id="S3.I2.i2.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> enlarges the dictionary <math id="S3.I2.i2.p1.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k\times k}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S\in\mathbb{R}^{R\times k\times k}</annotation></semantics></math> and thus increases <em id="S3.I2.i2.p1.5.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">spatial</em> expressivity in the kernel reconstruction <math id="S3.I2.i2.p1.4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W=MS" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>S</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W=MS</annotation></semantics></math> (Eq. (<a href="#S2.E22" title="In Equivalent matrix formulation. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S22</span></a>)). Even with perfect mixing, a small <math id="S3.I2.i2.p1.5.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> limits the diversity of spatial filters that can be expressed.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.6" class="ltx_p">Consequently, <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> play complementary roles: <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math> controls how flexibly PQKD can represent channel-to-channel mixing coefficients, whereas <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> controls how flexibly it can represent spatial kernel structure. Our sweep studies therefore treat <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(d,\dim(\theta))" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>,</mo><mrow><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(d,\dim(\theta))</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px8.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\{R_{\ell}\}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{R_{\ell}\}</annotation></semantics></math> as primary axes when constructing compression–accuracy frontiers (Sec. <a href="#S2.SS3" title="2.3 Scaling compression from partial to full convolutional compression ‣ 2 Results ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">2.3</span></a>).</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Connection to the photonic quantum feature map.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.5" class="ltx_p">In PQKD, the vector <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>z</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z</annotation></semantics></math> is not a free optimisation variable but is obtained as <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)=\Phi(\widehat{p}_{\theta})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mover accent="true"><mi>p</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)=\Phi(\widehat{p}_{\theta})</annotation></semantics></math> from shot-limited samples (Supplementary Note <a href="#S2.SS1a" title="S2.1 Photonic quantum feature map ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S2.1</span></a>). Thus, Eq. (<a href="#S3.E42" title="In Best achievable approximation to a target mixing. ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S42</span></a>) characterises an <em id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.5.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">idealised best case</em>: it describes the closest mixing achievable if <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>z</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z</annotation></semantics></math> could be chosen arbitrarily in <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathbb{R}^{d}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>d</mi></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{R}^{d}</annotation></semantics></math>. In practice, the attainable set is further constrained by the photonic map <math id="S3.SS1.SSS0.Px9.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta\mapsto z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta\mapsto z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> and finite-shot variability; these effects are investigated empirically via shot and noise sweeps (Sec. <a href="#S2.SS4" title="2.4 Robustness to shot noise and hardware-relevant perturbations ‣ 2 Results ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">2.4</span></a>).</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS2" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S3.2 </span>Approximation within the mixing subspace</h3>

<div id="S3.SS2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS2.p1.4" class="ltx_p">Fix the basis <math id="S3.SS2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="B" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>B</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math> and consider any target mixing tensor <math id="S3.SS2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M^{\star}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>M</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M^{\star}</annotation></semantics></math>. Under Eq. (<a href="#S3.E38" title="In Mixing subspace induced by a fixed generator. ‣ S3.1 Trainable-parameter accounting ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S38</span></a>), the best achievable mixing corresponds to the least-squares projection of <math id="S3.SS2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})</annotation></semantics></math> onto the column space of <math id="S3.SS2.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math>:</p>
<table id="S3.E43" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E43.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z^{\star}=\arg\min_{z\in\mathbb{R}^{d}}\ \left\|\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})-Az\right\|_{2}^{2},\quad\Rightarrow\quad Az^{\star}=\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}\,\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><msup><mi>z</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>arg</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mrow><munder><mi>min</mi><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mi>d</mi></msup></mrow></munder><mo>⁡</mo><msubsup><mrow><mo>‖</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow></mrow><mo>‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="0.889em">,</mo><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo></mrow></mrow><mspace style="width:1em;" width="1em"></mspace><mrow><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>z</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Π</mi><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mo>⋆</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z^{\star}=\arg\min_{z\in\mathbb{R}^{d}}\ \left\|\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star})-Az\right\|_{2}^{2},\quad\Rightarrow\quad Az^{\star}=\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}\,\mathrm{vec}(M^{\star}),</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S43)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS2.p1.8" class="ltx_p">where <math id="S3.SS2.p1.5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">Π</mi><mrow><mi>Range</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Pi_{\mathrm{Range}(A)}</annotation></semantics></math> denotes orthogonal projection. This characterises how <math id="S3.SS2.p1.6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="d" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>d</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math> and the choice of <math id="S3.SS2.p1.7.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> control the representational subspace for channel mixing, while <math id="S3.SS2.p1.8.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>R</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math> controls the spatial expressivity through the basis filters.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS3" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S3.3 </span>Finite-shot noise propagation</h3>

<div id="S3.SS3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS3.p1.4" class="ltx_p">The photonic feature vector <math id="S3.SS3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> is computed from a finite number of measurement shots. Consequently, the PQKD student does not receive the exact distributional feature <math id="S3.SS3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)=\Phi(p_{\theta})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)=\Phi(p_{\theta})</annotation></semantics></math>, but rather an empirical estimate <math id="S3.SS3.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\widehat{z}(\theta)=\Phi(\widehat{p}_{\theta})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mover accent="true"><mi>p</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\widehat{z}(\theta)=\Phi(\widehat{p}_{\theta})</annotation></semantics></math> constructed from <math id="S3.SS3.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> i.i.d. samples. This section formalises how finite-shot fluctuations propagate through the feature map and into the reconstructed convolution kernels, providing a principled basis for the noise studies reported in Sec. <a href="#S2.SS3" title="2.3 Scaling compression from partial to full convolutional compression ‣ 2 Results ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">2.3</span></a>.</p>
</div>
<section id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Concentration of the empirical measurement distribution.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.8" class="ltx_p">Let <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\widehat{p}_{\theta}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mover accent="true"><mi>p</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>θ</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\widehat{p}_{\theta}</annotation></semantics></math> be the empirical histogram over outcomes <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\omega\in\Omega" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>ω</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega\in\Omega</annotation></semantics></math> formed from <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> independent samples <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\omega_{1},\dots,\omega_{S}\sim p_{\theta}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>ω</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>ω</mi><mi>S</mi></msub></mrow><mo>∼</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega_{1},\dots,\omega_{S}\sim p_{\theta}</annotation></semantics></math>. For any fixed bin <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\omega" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>ω</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\omega</annotation></semantics></math>, the random variable <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\widehat{p}_{\theta}(\omega)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mover accent="true"><mi>p</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ω</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\widehat{p}_{\theta}(\omega)</annotation></semantics></math> is the sample mean of Bernoulli trials with mean <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p_{\theta}(\omega)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ω</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_{\theta}(\omega)</annotation></semantics></math>. Hoeffding’s inequality yields, for any <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.8.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\epsilon&gt;0" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>ϵ</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\epsilon&gt;0</annotation></semantics></math>,</p>
<table id="S3.E44" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E44.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathbb{P}\!\left(\left|\widehat{p}_{\theta}(\omega)-p_{\theta}(\omega)\right|\geq\epsilon\right)\leq 2\exp\!\left(-2S\epsilon^{2}\right)." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mpadded style="width:0.441em;" width="0.441em"><mi>ℙ</mi></mpadded><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mrow><msub><mover accent="true"><mi>p</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ω</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>ω</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>≥</mo><mi>ϵ</mi></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>≤</mo><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0.167em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mpadded style="width:1.370em;" width="1.370em"><mi>exp</mi></mpadded><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>S</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>ϵ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{P}\!\left(\left|\widehat{p}_{\theta}(\omega)-p_{\theta}(\omega)\right|\geq\epsilon\right)\leq 2\exp\!\left(-2S\epsilon^{2}\right).</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S44)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.9" class="ltx_p">This makes explicit the <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px1.p1.9.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1/\sqrt{S}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>/</mo><msqrt><mi>S</mi></msqrt></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1/\sqrt{S}</annotation></semantics></math> scaling of shot noise at the level of individual histogram entries.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">From histogram noise to feature noise.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.5" class="ltx_p">The photonic feature is obtained via a deterministic map <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\Phi" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Phi</annotation></semantics></math> applied to the empirical histogram: <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\widehat{z}(\theta)=\Phi(\widehat{p}_{\theta})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mover accent="true"><mi>p</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\widehat{z}(\theta)=\Phi(\widehat{p}_{\theta})</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)=\Phi(p_{\theta})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>θ</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)=\Phi(p_{\theta})</annotation></semantics></math>. Suppose <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\Phi" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi mathvariant="normal">Φ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\Phi</annotation></semantics></math> is Lipschitz with respect to the <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px2.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ell_{1}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ell_{1}</annotation></semantics></math> norm on histograms, i.e.,</p>
<table id="S3.E45" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">

Applying Eq. (<a href="#S3.E45" title="In From histogram noise to feature noise. ‣ S3.3 Finite-shot noise propagation ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S45</span></a>) gives</p>

</section>
<section id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Propagation to mixing coefficients and convolution kernels.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.3" class="ltx_p">In PQKD, the mixing tensor is generated linearly from the feature:</p>
<table id="S3.E49" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E49.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M)=Az,\qquad\mathrm{vec}(\widehat{M})=A\widehat{z}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>M</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>^</mo></mover></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M)=Az,\qquad\mathrm{vec}(\widehat{M})=A\widehat{z},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S49)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.4" class="ltx_p">so the induced perturbation obeys</p>
<table id="S3.E50" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E50.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\|\mathrm{vec}(\widehat{M})-\mathrm{vec}(M)\|_{2}\leq\|A\|_{2}\,\|\widehat{z}-z\|_{2}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>M</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>≤</mo><mrow><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo>−</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|\mathrm{vec}(\widehat{M})-\mathrm{vec}(M)\|_{2}\leq\|A\|_{2}\,\|\widehat{z}-z\|_{2}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S50)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Next, the reconstructed kernel satisfies <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W=MB" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W=MB</annotation></semantics></math> in the flattened formulation (Eq. (<a href="#S2.E22" title="In Equivalent matrix formulation. ‣ S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S22</span></a>)). Using submultiplicativity of operator norms, one obtains a Lipschitz bound for the kernel perturbation:</p>
<table id="S3.E51" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S3.E51.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\|W(B,\widehat{z})-W(B,z)\|_{F}=\|\widehat{M}B-MB\|_{F}\leq\|\widehat{M}-M\|_{F}\,\|B\|_{2}\leq\|A\|_{2}\,\|B\|_{F}\,\|\widehat{z}-z\|_{2}." display="block" accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>W</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mi>F</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mrow><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>M</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mi>F</mi></msub><mo>≤</mo><mrow><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mrow><mover stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mi>F</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em"
