encoding="application/x-tex">\|W(B,\widehat{z})-W(B,z)\|_{F}=\|\widehat{M}B-MB\|_{F}\leq\|\widehat{M}-M\|_{F}\,\|B\|_{2}\leq\|A\|_{2}\,\|B\|_{F}\,\|\widehat{z}-z\|_{2}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S51)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.2" class="ltx_p">where the final inequality uses <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px3.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\|B\|_{2}\leq\|S\|_{F}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>≤</mo><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mi>F</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|B\|_{2}\leq\|S\|_{F}</annotation></semantics></math> and the relationship between Frobenius and Euclidean norms under vectorisation.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Implications for training stability and noise studies.</h5>

<div id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.5" class="ltx_p">Equations (<a href="#S3.E48" title="In From histogram noise to feature noise. ‣ S3.3 Finite-shot noise propagation ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S48</span></a>)–(<a href="#S3.E51" title="In Propagation to mixing coefficients and convolution kernels. ‣ S3.3 Finite-shot noise propagation ‣ S3 Supplementary Note 3: Theory—expressivity, approximation, and stability ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S51</span></a>) show that the effective kernel noise induced by finite shots scales approximately as <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{K/S})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">𝒪</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msqrt><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>S</mi></mrow></msqrt><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{K/S})</annotation></semantics></math>, amplified by the projection magnitude <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\|A\|_{2}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|A\|_{2}</annotation></semantics></math> and the basis energy <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\|B\|_{F}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mrow><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">‖</mo></mrow><mi>F</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\|B\|_{F}</annotation></semantics></math>. This motivates two practical considerations that we evaluate empirically: (i) increasing <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>S</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math> reduces stochasticity in the photonic conditioning signal, and (ii) variance-reduction strategies such as feature smoothing (e.g., EMA in Supplementary Note <a href="#S6" title="S6 Supplementary Note 8: Training protocol ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S6</span></a>) can reduce the high-frequency fluctuations of <math id="S3.SS3.SSS0.Px4.p1.5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\widehat{z}(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\widehat{z}(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>, thereby stabilising both the induced kernels and the downstream student optimisation. These predictions are directly tested in the shot and noise impact experiments in the Sec. <a href="#S2.SS4" title="2.4 Robustness to shot noise and hardware-relevant perturbations ‣ 2 Results ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">2.4</span></a>.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S4a" class="ltx_section">
<h2 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">S4 </span>Supplementary Note 5: Classical models and baselines</h2>

<div id="S4a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4a.p1.1" class="ltx_p">This Supplementary Note specifies the classical teacher and student architectures used to evaluate PQKD, together with the baseline models required for fair attribution. Our design principle is to control for confounding factors: the teacher and PQKD student share the same high-level topology (number of convolutional blocks, pooling schedule, and classifier head), and we vary <em id="S4a.p1.1.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">only</em> the parameterisation of selected convolutional kernels and the source of the conditioning signal. This ensures that observed performance differences can be attributed to structured compression and photonic conditioning, rather than to unrelated architectural changes.</p>
</div>
<section id="S4.SS1a" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S4.1 </span>Teacher CNN (global-average-pooling head)</h3>

<div id="S4.SS1a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1a.p1.2" class="ltx_p">The teacher network is a conventional convolutional classifier with three convolutional blocks and a global-average-pooling (GAP) head<cite class="ltx_cite ltx_citemacro_cite">[<span class="ltx_ref ltx_missing_citation ltx_ref_self">lin2013network</span>]</cite>, chosen for (i) strong performance on MNIST/CIFAR-10 without excessive depth, (ii) stable training under standard optimisers, and (iii) compatibility with structured compression of the convolutional stack. Let <math id="S4.SS1a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C_{\mathrm{in}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{\mathrm{in}}</annotation></semantics></math> denote the input channels and let <math id="S4.SS1a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})</annotation></semantics></math> denote the channel widths.</p>
</div>
<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1a" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Architecture.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px1a.p1.1" class="ltx_p">The teacher consists of:</p>
<ul id="S4.I1a" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="S4.I1.i1a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i1a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i1a.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I1.i1a.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">conv1:</span> <math id="S4.I1.i1a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C_{\mathrm{in}}\rightarrow c_{1}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C_{\mathrm{in}}\rightarrow c_{1}</annotation></semantics></math> with <math id="S4.I1.i1a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="5\times 5" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>5</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>5</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">5\times 5</annotation></semantics></math> kernels, padding 2, followed by ReLU and <math id="S4.I1.i1a.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="2\times 2" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2\times 2</annotation></semantics></math> max-pooling.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I1.i2a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i2a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i2a.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I1.i2a.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">conv2:</span> <math id="S4.I1.i2a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c_{1}\rightarrow c_{2}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_{1}\rightarrow c_{2}</annotation></semantics></math> with <math id="S4.I1.i2a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="3\times 3" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>3</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3\times 3</annotation></semantics></math> kernels, padding 1, followed by ReLU and <math id="S4.I1.i2a.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="2\times 2" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2\times 2</annotation></semantics></math> max-pooling.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I1.i3a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i3a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i3a.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I1.i3a.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">conv3:</span> <math id="S4.I1.i3a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c_{2}\rightarrow c_{3}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_{2}\rightarrow c_{3}</annotation></semantics></math> with <math id="S4.I1.i3a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="3\times 3" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>3</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>3</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3\times 3</annotation></semantics></math> kernels, padding 1, followed by ReLU and dropout with <math id="S4.I1.i3a.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p=0.25" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0.25</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p=0.25</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I1.i4" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i4.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I1.i4.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">GAP:</span> adaptive average pooling to spatial size <math id="S4.I1.i4.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1\times 1" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1\times 1</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I1.i5" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I1.i5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I1.i5.p1.2" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I1.i5.p1.2.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Classifier:</span> a linear layer mapping <math id="S4.I1.i5.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="c_{3}\rightarrow C" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_{3}\rightarrow C</annotation></semantics></math> with <math id="S4.I1.i5.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C=10" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C=10</annotation></semantics></math> classes.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2a" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Teacher width sweep.</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2a.p1.1" class="ltx_p">To obtain clear compression ratios while maintaining a strong teacher reference, we sweep teacher widths over representative settings such as</p>
<table id="S4.E52" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E52.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})\in\{(32,64,128),\ (48,96,128),\ (64,128,128)\}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>32</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>64</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>48</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>96</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.667em">,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>64</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>128</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})\in\{(32,64,128),\ (48,96,128),\ (64,128,128)\},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S52)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px2a.p1.2" class="ltx_p">and report teacher accuracy and parameter counts for each setting. In all cases, the teacher is trained to convergence (or a fixed epoch budget) using standard cross-entropy on hard labels.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3a" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Teacher parameter count (convolutional stack).</h5>

<div id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3a.p1.3" class="ltx_p">For completeness, the number of trainable parameters in the three convolutional layers is</p>
<table id="S4.E53" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E53.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{teacher,conv}}=\sum_{\ell=1}^{3}\Big(C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}C_{\mathrm{in}}^{(\ell)}k_{\ell}^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}\Big)," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mrow><mi>teacher</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>conv</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false" rspace="0em">∑</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mn>3</mn></munderover><mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">(</mo><mrow><mrow><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>in</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>k</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mrow><mo>+</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo maxsize="1.600em" minsize="1.600em">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{teacher,conv}}=\sum_{\ell=1}^{3}\Big(C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}C_{\mathrm{in}}^{(\ell)}k_{\ell}^{2}+C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(\ell)}\Big),</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S53)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3a.p1.2" class="ltx_p">with <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(k_{1},k_{2},k_{3})=(5,3,3)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>5</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>3</mn><mo>,</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(k_{1},k_{2},k_{3})=(5,3,3)</annotation></semantics></math> and <math id="S4.SS1.SSS0.Px3a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(1)},C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(2)},C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(3)})=(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>,</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo>,</mo><msubsup><mi>C</mi><mi>out</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(1)},C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(2)},C_{\mathrm{out}}^{(3)})=(c_{1},c_{2},c_{3})</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS2a" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S4.2 </span>Student architectures</h3>

<div id="S4.SS2a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS2a.p1.3" class="ltx_p">The PQKD student matches the teacher macro-architecture (same block structure and GAP head) but replaces selected convolutional layers by photonic-conditioned dictionary convolutions (Supplementary Note <a href="#S2.SS2a" title="S2.2 Photonic-conditioned dictionary convolution ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S2.2</span></a>). Concretely, for each compressed convolution layer <math id="S4.SS2a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ell\in\mathcal{L}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ell\in\mathcal{L}</annotation></semantics></math>, the dense kernel is replaced by a trainable spatial basis <math id="S4.SS2a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S^{(\ell)}\in\mathbb{R}^{R_{\ell}\times k_{\ell}\times k_{\ell}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S^{(\ell)}\in\mathbb{R}^{R_{\ell}\times k_{\ell}\times k_{\ell}}</annotation></semantics></math> and a photonic-generated mixing tensor <math id="S4.SS2a.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math>:</p>
<table id="S4.E54" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E54.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:},\qquad\ell\in\mathcal{L}." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>vec</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mrow><msubsup><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><munderover><mo movablelimits="false">∑</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi></msub></munderover><mrow><msubsup><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msubsup><mi>S</mi><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>,</mo><mo rspace="0em">:</mo><mo>,</mo><mo>:</mo></mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msubsup></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="2.167em">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{vec}(M^{(\ell)})=A^{(\ell)}z(\theta),\qquad W^{(\ell)}_{o,i,:,:}=\sum_{r=1}^{R_{\ell}}M^{(\ell)}_{o,i,r}\,S^{(\ell)}_{r,:,:},\qquad\ell\in\mathcal{L}.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S54)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.SS2a.p1.4" class="ltx_p">Layers not in <math id="S4.SS2a.p1.4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathcal{L}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">ℒ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{L}</annotation></semantics></math> remain standard dense convolutions with fully trainable kernels. We evaluate three compression configurations (Supplementary Note <a href="#S2.SS3a" title="S2.3 Compression configurations ‣ S2 Supplementary Note 2: Definition of Photonic Quantum Knowledge Distillation ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S2.3</span></a>): compress <span id="S4.SS2a.p1.4.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv1</span> only; compress <span id="S4.SS2a.p1.4.2" class="ltx_text ltx_font_typewriter">conv1+conv2</span>; and compress all convolution layers.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS3a" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S4.3 </span>Baselines and controls</h3>

<div id="S4.SS3a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3a.p1.1" class="ltx_p">Because PQKD combines two ingredients—structured parameterisation and a photonic conditioning signal—we include baseline models that isolate each factor. The goal is to distinguish: (i) gains attributable to distillation alone, (ii) gains attributable to dictionary structure alone, and (iii) gains attributable specifically to photonic-conditioned parameter generation.</p>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS3a.p2" class="ltx_para">
<ol id="S4.I2a" class="ltx_enumerate">
<li id="S4.I2.i1a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">1.</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i1a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i1a.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i1a.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">KD-only student (no compression).</span>
A student with reduced width (or identical architecture) trained using the distillation objective in Eq. (<a href="#S1.E2" title="In S1.1 Knowledge distillation ‣ S1 Supplementary Note 1: Fundamentals ‣ Photonic Quantum-Enhanced Knowledge Distillation" class="ltx_ref"><span class="ltx_text ltx_ref_tag">S2</span></a>), without replacing any convolution kernels. This baseline quantifies the benefit of knowledge distillation absent structured compression.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i2a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">2.</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i2a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i2a.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i2a.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Dictionary-only student (no photonic conditioning).</span>
Replace the target convolution layers by the same dictionary decomposition
<math id="S4.I2.i2a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="W_{o,i}=\sum_{r}M_{o,i,r}S_{r}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>W</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi></mrow></msub><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><msub><mo>∑</mo><mi>r</mi></msub><mrow><msub><mi>M</mi><mrow><mi>o</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>i</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mi>r</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">W_{o,i}=\sum_{r}M_{o,i,r}S_{r}</annotation></semantics></math>, but treat <math id="S4.I2.i2a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>M</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M</annotation></semantics></math> as a <em id="S4.I2.i2a.p1.3.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">trainable</em> parameter tensor rather than generating it from <math id="S4.I2.i2a.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>. This isolates the effect of the dictionary factorisation while removing the photonic control constraint.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i3a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">3.</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i3a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i3a.p1.3" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i3a.p1.3.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Random-feature conditioning.</span>
Replace the photonic feature <math id="S4.I2.i3a.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> by i.i.d. Gaussian features <math id="S4.I2.i3a.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\tilde{z}\sim\mathcal{N}(0,I_{d})" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>z</mi><mo>~</mo></mover><mo>∼</mo><mrow><mi class="ltx_font_mathcaligraphic">𝒩</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mi>d</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\tilde{z}\sim\mathcal{N}(0,I_{d})</annotation></semantics></math> (optionally re-sampled per epoch or fixed per run), while keeping the same fixed projection <math id="S4.I2.i3a.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>A</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math> and dictionary basis parameterisation. This baseline tests whether PQKD improvements could be explained by generic stochastic conditioning rather than photonic structure.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I2.i4a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">4.</span> 
<div id="S4.I2.i4a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.4" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Fixed photonic feature (no <math id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> learning).</span>
Use the photonic sampling and feature map to compute <math id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="z(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math> but keep <math id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> fixed throughout training (no SPSA or other updates). This baseline isolates the value of <em id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.4.2" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">learning</em> <math id="S4.I2.i4a.p1.4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> as opposed to using a static photonic feature.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS3a.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS3a.p3.1" class="ltx_p">When reporting results, we keep training budgets (epochs, batch sizes, optimiser settings) identical across PQKD and baselines unless explicitly stated, and we use the same teacher checkpoint for all student variants in a given experimental run.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S4.SS4a" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S4.4 </span>Parameter counting conventions</h3>

<div id="S4.SS4a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS4a.p1.1" class="ltx_p">We report compression ratios under two complementary conventions to avoid ambiguity:</p>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS4a.p2" class="ltx_para">
<ul id="S4.I3a" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="S4.I3.i1a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I3.i1a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I3.i1a.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I3.i1a.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Overall trainable-parameter ratio:</span></p>
<table id="S4.E55" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E55.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{overall}}=\frac{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{teacher}}}{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}}\quad\text{with $\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}$ including }\dim(\theta)\text{ once.}" display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>CR</mi><mi>overall</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mfrac><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>teacher</mi></msub></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>student</mi></msub></mrow></mfrac><mspace style="width:1em;" width="1em"></mspace><mrow><mrow><mtext>with </mtext><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mi>student</mi></msub></mrow><mtext> including </mtext></mrow><mo lspace="0.167em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mtext> once.</mtext></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{overall}}=\frac{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{teacher}}}{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}}\quad\text{with $\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student}}$ including }\dim(\theta)\text{ once.}</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S55)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
</div>
</li>
<li id="S4.I3.i2a" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="S4.I3.i2a.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.I3.i2a.p1.1" class="ltx_p"><span id="S4.I3.i2a.p1.1.1" class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Conv-only ratio:</span></p>
<table id="S4.E56" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S4.E56.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{conv}}=\frac{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{teacher,conv}}}{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student,conv}}}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>CR</mi><mi>conv</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mrow><mi>teacher</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>conv</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">#</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>params</mi><mrow><mi>student</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>conv</mi></mrow></msub></mrow></mfrac></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{CR}_{\mathrm{conv}}=\frac{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{teacher,conv}}}{\#\mathrm{params}_{\mathrm{student,conv}}},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S56)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S4.I3.i2a.p1.2" class="ltx_p">computed by restricting the parameter count to convolutional layers only. This isolates compression achieved in the feature extractor independent of the classifier head.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div id="S4.SS4a.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S4.SS4a.p3.2" class="ltx_p">Fixed projection matrices <math id="S4.SS4a.p3.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="A^{(\ell)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>A</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">ℓ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A^{(\ell)}</annotation></semantics></math> are excluded from all trainable-parameter counts because they are not optimised; however, they may contribute to memory footprint and can be implemented in structured form if required. Photonic parameters <math id="S4.SS4a.p3.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> are included in the student trainable budget by default (unless explicitly stated otherwise) to reflect the full learnable budget of the PQKD mechanism.</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="S5" class="ltx_section">
<h2 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">S5 </span>Supplementary Note 7: Quantum model details</h2>

<section id="S5.SS1" class="ltx_subsection">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">S5.1 </span>Circuit family and theta-length constraint</h3>

<div id="S5.SS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S5.SS1.p1.3" class="ltx_p">Our PQKD implementation interfaces with a programmable CV photonic sampler whose native parameterisation is tied to a specific interferometric circuit family. In particular, the backend adopts a <em id="S5.SS1.p1.3.1" class="ltx_emph ltx_font_italic">tiled</em> interferometer structure consistent with loop- or time-bin architectures, where each “tiling” (or layer) implements a fixed-pattern mode mixing described by a sequence of beam-splitter operations interleaved with phase shifts. Within this circuit family, the number of independent mixing angles per tiling scales linearly with the number of modes <math id="S5.SS1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>N</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math>, rather than quadratically as in a fully general <math id="S5.SS1.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="U(N)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>U</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>N</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U(N)</annotation></semantics></math> mesh. This architectural choice reflects realistic constraints of compact photonic implementations (e.g., single-loop interferometers), and it directly determines the admissible length of the continuous parameter vector <math id="S5.SS1.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>θ</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta</annotation></semantics></math> accepted by the sampler.</p>
</div>
<section id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Per-tiling parameter count.</h5>

<div id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.1" class="ltx_p">For an <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>N</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N</annotation></semantics></math>-mode instance, a single tiling is parameterised by</p>
<table id="S5.E57" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S5.E57.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="L_{\mathrm{tile}}=N-1" display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>tile</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L_{\mathrm{tile}}=N-1</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S57)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2" class="ltx_p">real-valued angles associated with beam-splitter reflectivities (and/or equivalent mixing parameters) in the fixed connectivity pattern of the backend. For the main experiments with <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N=16" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>16</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">N=16</annotation></semantics></math> modes, this implies</p>
<table id="S5.E58" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S5.E58.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="L_{\mathrm{tile}}=N-1=15." display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>tile</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>15</mn></mrow><mo lspace="0em">.</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L_{\mathrm{tile}}=N-1=15.</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S58)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.4" class="ltx_p">We denote by <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta^{(t)}\in\mathbb{R}^{L_{\mathrm{tile}}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>tile</mi></msub></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta^{(t)}\in\mathbb{R}^{L_{\mathrm{tile}}}</annotation></semantics></math> the parameter vector controlling tiling <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px1.p1.4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="t" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mi>t</mi><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Tiling interpretation for extended parameter vectors.</h5>

<div id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.4" class="ltx_p">To support systematic sweeps over the effective photonic parameter budget <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)</annotation></semantics></math>, we allow user-specified vectors whose length may exceed <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="L_{\mathrm{tile}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>tile</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L_{\mathrm{tile}}</annotation></semantics></math>. When <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\dim(\theta)&gt;L_{\mathrm{tile}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>&gt;</mo><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>tile</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\dim(\theta)&gt;L_{\mathrm{tile}}</annotation></semantics></math>, the backend interprets the circuit as a concatenation of multiple identical connectivity tiles, each with its own set of <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(N-1)" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(N-1)</annotation></semantics></math> parameters. Specifically, we define the number of tiles as</p>
<table id="S5.E59" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S5.E59.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n_{\mathrm{tiling}}=\left\lceil\frac{\dim(\theta)}{N-1}\right\rceil," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>tiling</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>⌈</mo><mfrac><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mfrac><mo>⌉</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n_{\mathrm{tiling}}=\left\lceil\frac{\dim(\theta)}{N-1}\right\rceil,</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S59)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.7" class="ltx_p">so that the circuit consumes a total of</p>
<table id="S5.E60" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>

<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>
<td rowspan="1" class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_eqno ltx_align_middle ltx_align_right"><span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_equation ltx_align_right">(S60)</span></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.8" class="ltx_p">angles. Conceptually, this corresponds to composing the interferometer as a product</p>
<table id="S5.E61" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">

<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S5.E61.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="U(\theta_{\mathrm{fit}})=U^{(n_{\mathrm{tiling}})}(\theta^{(n_{\mathrm{tiling}})})\cdots U^{(2)}(\theta^{(2)})U^{(1)}(\theta^{(1)})," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>U</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mi>fit</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>U</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>tiling</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>tiling</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⋯</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>U</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msup><mi>U</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">​</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U(\theta_{\mathrm{fit}})=U^{(n_{\mathrm{tiling}})}(\theta^{(n_{\mathrm{tiling}})})\cdots U^{(2)}(\theta^{(2)})U^{(1)}(\theta^{(1)}),</annotation></semantics></math></td>

<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.6" class="ltx_p">where each <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="U^{(t)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msup><mi>U</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">U^{(t)}</annotation></semantics></math> is a single-tiling interferometric transformation parameterised by <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px2.p1.6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta^{(t)}\in\mathbb{R}^{N-1}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>θ</mi><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msup><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta^{(t)}\in\mathbb{R}^{N-1}</annotation></semantics></math>.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px3" class="ltx_paragraph">
<h5 class="ltx_title ltx_title_paragraph">Deterministic adjustment for sampler compatibility.</h5>

<div id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.2" class="ltx_p">Because the sampler expects exactly <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="L_{\mathrm{eff}}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>eff</mi></msub><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L_{\mathrm{eff}}</annotation></semantics></math> parameters, we map the user-specified <math id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta\in\mathbb{R}^{\dim(\theta)}" display="inline" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mi>θ</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mo rspace="0em">dim</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta\in\mathbb{R}^{\dim(\theta)}</annotation></semantics></math> to a backend-compatible vector</p>
<table id="S5.E62" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_left"><math id="S5.E62.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\theta\mapsto\theta_{\mathrm{fit}}\in\mathbb{R}^{(N-1)\,n_{\mathrm{tiling}}}," display="block" intent=":literal"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><msub><mi>θ</mi><mi>fit</mi></msub><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>ℝ</mi><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0.170em" rspace="0em">​</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>tiling</mi></msub></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>,</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\theta\mapsto\theta_{\mathrm{fit}}\in\mathbb{R}^{(N-1)\,n_{\mathrm{tiling}}},</annotation></semantics></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_left_padright"></td>

<p id="S5.SS1.SSS0.Px3.p1.5" class="ltx_p">using a deterministic rule that preserves reproducibility:</p>

class="ltx_mathvariant_bold" mathvariant="bold"> 0</mn><mo maxsize="1.200em" minsize="1.200em">]</mo></mrow></mtd><mtd class="ltx_align_left" columnalign="left"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mtext>if </mtext><mo \theta_{1:L_{\mathrm{eff}}}&amp;\text{if }\dim(\theta)&gt;L_{\mathrm{eff}}\quad\text{(truncation)},\\[4.0pt]
